 CAG Report 2018: sieji(cag report) ne narendra modi sarkaar(narendra Modi Government)ke vittiya prabandhan par bada khulaasa kiya he
 According to the CAG report, the Modi government has spent more than four lakh crore rupees to hide the debt and borrowings
 is dhanrashi kaa zikr bajet ke dastavejon main nahin he
 It is believed that the government used the method of off-budget financing to keep the indicators and figures of the fiscal deficit correct

 82 varshiya mahila kanchan devi baid santhara lene kii vajah se surkhiyon main aa gai hai
 According to the traditions of Jainism, the person taking santhara boycott food and drink till death
 jain dharm ke log is vrath ko festival of deth kehete hai
 Let's know about 5 important things related to Santhara
 1
 The person taking the santhara is forced to stop eating or he voluntarily abandons it
 aksar mrityu ko kareeb dekhne ke baad hi vyakti ise lene kaa faisla karata he
 2
 jain granthon kii manyataon ke anusaar santhara main niyam ke mutabik hi vyakti ko bhojan diya jaataa he
 The decision to stop food is taken only when digestion of food is not possible
 3
 There are two ways to fast in Santhara
 ise lene vaale vyakti par yah nirbhar karata he ki vah santhara ke dauraan pani pinaa chahta he yaa nahin
 In this, any kind of food is completely excluded
